search help getting started the inline xbrl viewer allows user to quickly easily review detail of the tagged information in inline document automatically placing top and bottom highlight border around tagged numeric fact and left and right border each block tagged fact hovering over tagged fact will highlight shade all content related to the tagged fact and clicking on tagged fact will reveal tagging detail in the fact review window navigation search and filter option also provided to easily refine and identify specific type of tagged information fact review window the fact review window show the tagging detail for the currently selected fact is highlighted solid blue border are four category of fact detail which can be viewed an value indicates there is available information for the item within the given category attribute all primary information applicable describing the tagged fact including period sign decimal dimensional detail ax and member scale measure and data type label detailed documentation definition for the tag used and label reference authoritative reference information applicable for the selected tag calculation balance and calculation hierarchy detail numeric result search operator and via and and or via or or are available to refine search fact the search fact box can be used to find tagged fact matching entered keywords by default tag name tag label and the magnifying glass icon to clear the search the content included in search can be increased to included tag definition dimension and authoritative reference by selecting the cog wheel icon to the left of the search box see setting for more information section the search section box can be used to filter the tagged section of the financial statement filter filter change the number of highlighted fact and item in the fact list by providing several way to review and pinpoint certain tagged information multiple filter can be used data filter these filter option allow the user to among other thing invoke the orderly liquidation authority instead of the bankruptcy code if the secretary of the treasury make certain financial distress and systemic risk determination the orderly liquidation authority is modeled in part on the federal deposit insurance act but also adopts certain concept from the bankruptcy code the orderly liquidation authority contains certain difference from the bankruptcy code for example in certain circumstance the fdic could permit payment of obligation it determines to be systemically significant short term creditor or operating creditor in lieu of paying other obligation long term creditor without the need to obtain creditor consent or prior court review the insolvency and resolution process could also lead to large reduction or total bhc with bridge holding company which could continue operation and result in an orderly resolution of the underlying bank but whose equity is held solely for the benefit of creditor of the original bhc furthermore the federal reserve requires that bhcs maintain minimum level of long term debt required to provide adequate loss absorbing capacity in the event of resolution for more information financial institution in the the volcker rulethe volcker rule prohibits insured depository institution and company affiliated with insured depository institution collectively banking entity from relationship with hedge fund and private equity fund the volcker rule provides exemption for certain activity including market making underwriting hedging trading in government obligation insurance company activity and organizing and offering hedge fund and private equity fund the volcker rule also clarifies that certain activity are not prohibited including acting agent broker or custodian banking entity with significant trading operation such the corporation is required to maintain detailed compliance program to comply with the restriction of the volcker rule derivativesour derivative both period included income tax benefit adjustment to eliminate the fte treatment of certain tax credit recorded in global banking and global market managing riskrisk is inherent in all our business activity sound risk management enables to serve our customer and deliver for our shareholder if not managed well risk can result in financial loss regulatory sanction and penalty and damage to our reputation each of which may adversely impact our ability to execute our business strategy we take comprehensive approach to risk management with defined risk framework and an articulated risk appetite statement which are approved annually by the erc and the board the seven key type of risk faced by the corporation are strategic credit market liquidity compliance operational and reputational strategic risk is the risk to current or projected financial condition arising from incorrect assumption about external or internal factor inappropriate business plan ineffective business strategy execution or failure to respond in timely manner to change in the regulatory macroeconomic or competitive environment in the geographic location in which we operate credit risk is the risk of loss arising from the inability or failure of borrower or counterparty to meet it obligation market risk is the risk that change in market condition adversely impact the value of asset or liability or otherwise negatively impact earnings market risk is composed of price risk and interest rate risk liquidity risk is the inability to meet expected or unexpected cash flow and collateral need while continuing to support our business and customer under range of economic condition compliance risk is the risk of legal or regulatory sanction material financial loss or damage to the reputation of the corporation arising from the failure of the corporation to comply with the requirement of applicable law rule and regulation and our internal policy and procedure operational risk is the risk of loss resulting from inadequate or failed internal process or system people or external event reputational risk is the risk that negative perception of the corporation may adversely impact profitability or operation the following section address in more detail the specific procedure measure and analysis of the major category of risk this discussion of managing risk focus on the current risk framework that part of it annual review process wa approved by the erc and the board set forth in our risk framework culture of managing risk well is fundamental to our value and our purpose and how we drive responsible growth it requires to focus on risk in all activity and encourages the necessary mindset and behavior to enable effective risk management and promote sound risk taking within our risk appetite sustaining culture of managing risk well throughout the organization is critical to the success of the corporation and is clear expectation of our executive management team and the board our risk framework serf the foundation for the consistent and effective management of risk facing the corporation the risk framework set forth role and responsibility for the management of risk and provides blueprint for how the board through delegation of authority to committee and executive officer establishes risk appetite and associated limit for our activity executive management ass with board oversight the risk adjusted return of each business management review and approves the strategic and financial operating plan well the capital plan and risk appetite statement and recommends them annually to the board for approval our strategic plan take into consideration return objective and financial resource which must align with risk capacity and risk appetite management set financial objective for each business by allocating capital and setting target for return on capital for each business capital allocation and operating limit are regularly evaluated part of our overall governance process the business and the economic environment in which we operate continue to evolve for more information regarding capital allocation see business segment operation on page the corporation risk appetite indicates the amount of capital earnings or liquidity we are willing to put at risk to achieve our strategic objective and business plan consistent with applicable regulatory requirement our risk appetite provides common framework that includes set of measure to assist senior management and the board in assessing the corporation risk profile against our risk appetite and risk capacity our risk appetite is formally articulated in the risk appetite statement which includes both qualitative statement and quantitative limit our overall capacity to take risk is limited therefore we prioritize the risk we take in order to maintain strong and flexible financial position so we can withstand challenging economic condition and take advantage of organic growth opportunity therefore we set objective and target for capital and liquidity that are intended to permit to continue to operate in safe and sound manner at all time including during period of stress our line of business operate with risk limit that align with the corporation risk appetite senior management is responsible for tracking and reporting performance measurement well any exception to risk appetite limit the board and it committee when appropriate oversee financial performance execution of the strategic and financial operating plan adherence to risk appetite limit and the adequacy of internal control for more detailed discussion of our risk management activity see the discussion below and page through risk management governancethe risk framework describes delegation of authority whereby the board and it committee may delegate authority to management level committee or executive officer such delegation may authorize certain decision making and approval function which may be evidenced in document such committee charter job description meeting minute and resolution the chart below illustrates the interrelationship among the board board committee and management committee that have the majority of risk oversight responsibility for the corporation bank of america of director and board committeesthe board is composed of director all but one of whom are independent the board integrated in key strategic capital and financial planning process and in day to day business process across the corporation thereby ensuring risk are appropriately considered evaluated and responded to in timely manner we employ an effective risk management process referred to identify measure monitor and control part of our daily activity identify to be effectively managed risk must be proactively identified and well understood proper risk identification focus on recognizing and understanding key risk inherent in our business activity or key risk that may arise from external factor each employee is expected to identify and escalate risk promptly risk identification is an ongoing process that incorporates input from flu and control function it is designed to be forward looking and to capture relevant risk factor across all of our line of business measure once risk is identified it must be prioritized and accurately measured through systematic process including qualitative statement and quantitative limit risk is measured at various level including but not limited to risk type flu and legal entity and also on an aggregate basis this risk measurement process help to capture change in our risk profile due to change in strategic direction concentration portfolio quality and the overall economic environment senior management considers how risk exposure might evolve under variety of stress scenario monitor we monitor risk level regularly to track adherence to risk appetite policy and standard we also regularly update risk assessment and review risk exposure through our monitoring we know our level of risk relative to limit and can take action in timely manner we also know when risk limit are breached and have process to appropriately report and escalate exception this includes timely request for approval to manager and alert to executive management management level committee or the board directly or through an appropriate committee control we establish and communicate risk limit and control through policy standard procedure and process the limit and control can be adjusted by senior management or the board when condition or risk tolerance warrant these limit may be absolute loan amount trading volume operational loss or relative percentage of loan book in higher risk category our flu are held accountable for performing within the established limit the formal process used to manage risk represent part of our overall risk management process we instill strong and comprehensive culture of managing risk well through communication training policy procedure and organizational role and responsibility establishing culture reflective of our purpose to help make our customer financial life better and delivering on responsible growth is also critical to effective risk management we are committed to the highest principle of ethical and professional conduct conduct risk is the risk of improper action behavior or practice by the corporation it employee or representative that are illegal unethical and or contrary to our core value that could result in harm to the corporation our shareholder or our customer damage the integrity of the financial market or negatively impact our reputation we have established protocol and structure so that conduct risk is governed and reported across the corporation appropriately all employee are held accountable for adhering to the code of conduct operating within our risk appetite and managing risk in their daily business activity in addition our performance management and compensation practice encourage responsible risk taking that is consistent with our risk framework and risk appetite corporation wide stress testingintegral to our capital planning financial planning and strategic planning process we conduct capital scenario management and stress forecasting on periodic basis to better understand balance sheet earnings and capital sensitivity to certain economic and business scenario including economic and market condition that are more severe than anticipated these stress forecast provide an understanding of the potential impact from our risk profile on the balance sheet earnings and capital and serve key component of our capital and risk management practice the intent of stress testing is to develop comprehensive understanding of potential impact of on and off balance sheet risk at the corporation and certain subsidiary and how they impact financial resiliency which provides confidence to management regulator and our investor contingency planningwe have developed and maintain contingency plan that are designed to prepare in advance to respond in the event of bank of america adverse economic financial or market stress these contingency plan include our capital contingency plan and financial contingency and recovery plan which provide monitoring escalation action and routine designed to enable to increase capital access funding source and reduce risk through consideration of potential option that include asset sale business sale capital or debt issuance and other de risking strategy we also maintain resolution plan to limit adverse systemic impact that could be associated with potential resolution of bank of america strategic risk managementstrategic risk is embedded in every business and is one of the major risk category along with credit market liquidity compliance operational and reputational risk this risk result from incorrect assumption about external or internal factor inappropriate business plan ineffective business strategy execution or failure to respond in timely manner to change in the regulatory macroeconomic or competitive environment in the geographic location in which we operate such competitor action changing customer preference product obsolescence and technology development an aspect of strategic risk is the risk that the corporation capital level are not adequate to meet minimum regulatory requirement and support execution of business activity or absorb loss from risk during normal or adverse economic and market condition such capital risk is managed in parallel to strategic risk we manage strategic risk through the strategic risk enterprise policy and integration into the strategic planning process among other activity our strategic plan is consistent with our risk appetite capital plan and liquidity requirement and specifically address strategic risk impacting each business on an annual basis the board review and approves the strategic plan capital plan financial operating plan and risk appetite statement with oversight by the board senior management directs the line of business to execute our strategic plan consistent with our core operating principle and risk appetite the executive management team monitor business performance throughout the year and provides the board with regular progress report on whether strategic objective and timeline are being met including report on strategic risk and if additional or alternative action need to be considered or implemented the regular executive review focus on assessing forecasted earnings and return on capital the current risk profile current capital and liquidity requirement staffing level and change required to support the strategic plan stress testing result and other qualitative factor such market growth rate and peer analysis significant strategic action such capital action material acquisition or divestiture and resolution plan are reviewed and approved by the board at the business where required with oversight by the board and the erc executive management performs similar analysis throughout the year and evaluates change to the financial forecast or the risk capital or liquidity position deemed appropriate to balance and optimize achieving the targeted risk appetite shareholder return and maintaining the targeted financial strength proprietary model are used to measure the capital requirement for credit country market operational and strategic risk the allocated capital assigned to each business is based on it unique risk profile with oversight by the board and transaction capital managementthe corporation manages it capital position so that it capital is more than adequate to support it business activity and aligns with risk risk appetite and strategic maintained net liquid asset at december that exceeded the applicable minimum requirement under the exchange act liquidity riskfunding and liquidity risk managementour primary liquidity risk management objective is to meet expected or unexpected cash flow and collateral requirement including payment under long term debt agreement commitment to extend credit and customer deposit withdrawal while continuing to support our business and customer under range of economic condition to achieve that objective we analyze and monitor our liquidity risk under expected and stressed condition maintain liquidity and access to diverse funding source including our stable deposit base and seek to align liquidity related incentive and risk these liquidity risk management practice have allowed to effectively manage the market fluctuation from the rising interest rate environment inflationary pressure and macroeconomic environment we define liquidity readily available asset limited to cash and high quality liquid unencumbered security that we can use to meet our contractual and contingent financial obligation they arise we manage our liquidity position through line of business and alm activity well through our legal entity funding strategy on both forward and current bank of america including intraday basis under both expected and stressed condition we believe that centralized approach to funding and liquidity management enhances our ability to monitor liquidity requirement maximizes access to funding source minimizes borrowing cost and facilitates timely response to liquidity event the board approves our liquidity risk policy and the financial contingency and recovery plan the erc establishes our liquidity risk tolerance level the mrc is responsible for overseeing liquidity risk and directing management to maintain exposure within the established tolerance level the mrc review and monitor our liquidity position and stress testing result approves certain liquidity risk limit and review the impact of strategic decision on our liquidity for more information see managing risk on page under this governance framework we developed certain funding and liquidity risk management practice which include maintaining liquidity at bank of america corporation parent and selected subsidiary including our bank subsidiary and other regulated entity condition diversifying funding source considering our asset profile and legal entity structure and performing contingency planning nb holding corporationthe parent which is separate and distinct legal financial statement credit risk managementcredit risk is the risk of loss arising from the inability or failure of borrower or counterparty to meet it obligation credit risk can also arise from operational failure that result in an erroneous advance commitment or investment of fund we define the credit exposure to borrower or counterparty the loss potential arising from all product classification including loan and lease deposit overdraft derivative asset held for sale and unfunded lending commitment which include loan commitment letter of credit and financial guarantee derivative position are recorded at fair value and asset held for sale are recorded at either fair value or the lower of cost or fair value certain loan and unfunded commitment are accounted for under the fair value option credit risk for category of asset carried at fair value is not accounted for part of the allowance for credit loss but part of the fair value adjustment recorded in earnings for derivative position our credit risk is measured the net cost in the event the counterparties with contract in which we are in gain position fail to perform under the term of those contract we use the current fair value to represent credit exposure without giving consideration to future mark to market change the credit risk amount take into consideration the effect of legally enforceable master netting agreement and cash collateral our consumer and commercial credit extension and review procedure encompass funded and unfunded credit exposure for more information on derivative and credit extension commitment see note derivative and note commitment and contingency to the consolidated financial statement we manage credit risk based on the risk profile of the borrower or counterparty repayment source the nature of underlying collateral and other support given current event condition and expectation we classify our portfolio either consumer or commercial and monitor credit risk in each discussed below we refine our underwriting and credit risk management practice well credit standard to meet the changing economic environment to mitigate loss and enhance customer support in our consumer business we have in place collection program and loan modification and customer assistance infrastructure we utilize number of action to mitigate loss in the commercial business including increasing the frequency and intensity of portfolio monitoring hedging activity and our practice of transferring management of deteriorating commercial exposure to independent special asset officer commercial portfolio credit risk managementcredit risk management for the commercial portfolio begin with an assessment of the credit risk profile of the borrower or counterparty based on an analysis of it financial position part of the overall credit risk assessment our commercial credit exposure are assigned risk rating and are subject to approval based on defined credit approval standard subsequent to loan origination risk rating are monitored on an ongoing basis and if necessary adjusted to reflect change in the financial condition cash flow risk profile or outlook of borrower or counterparty in making credit decision we consider risk rating collateral country industry and single name concentration limit while also balancing these consideration with the total borrower or counterparty relationship we use variety of tool to continuously monitor the ability of borrower or counterparty to perform under it obligation we use risk rating aggregation to measure and evaluate concentration within portfolio in addition risk rating are factor in determining the level of allocated capital and the allowance for credit loss part of our ongoing risk mitigation initiative we attempt to work with client experiencing financial difficulty to modify their loan to term that better align with their current ability to pay in situation where an economic concession ha been granted to borrower experiencing financial difficulty we identify these loan tdrs for more information on our accounting policy regarding delinquency nonperforming status and net charge offs for the exposure by region and by country table and summarize our concentration we also utilize syndication of exposure to third party loan sale hedging and other risk mitigation technique to manage the size accounted for under the fair value option primarily includes amount related to credit card and unsecured consumer lending portfolio in consumer banking bank of america risk managementmarket risk is the risk that change in market condition may adversely impact the value of asset or liability or otherwise negatively impact earnings this risk is inherent in the financial instrument associated with our operation primarily within our global market segment we are also exposed to these risk in other area of the corporation our alm activity in the event of market stress these risk could have material impact on our result for more information see interest rate risk management for the banking book on page our traditional banking loan and deposit product are non trading position and are generally reported at amortized cost for asset or the amount owed for liability historical cost however these position are still subject to change in economic value based on varying market condition with one of the primary risk being change in the level of interest rate the risk of adverse change in the economic value of our non trading position arising from change in interest rate is managed through our alm activity we have elected to account for certain asset and liability under the fair value option our trading position are reported at fair value with change reflected in income trading position are subject to various change in market based risk factor the majority of this risk is generated by our activity in the interest rate foreign exchange credit equity and commodity market in addition the value of asset and liability could change due to market liquidity correlation across market and expectation of market volatility we seek to manage these risk exposure by using variety of technique that encompass broad range of financial instrument the key risk management technique are discussed in more detail in the trading risk management section grm is responsible for providing senior management with clear and comprehensive understanding of the trading risk to which we are exposed these responsibility include ownership of market risk policy developing and maintaining quantitative risk model calculating aggregated risk measure establishing and monitoring position limit consistent with risk appetite conducting daily review and analysis of trading inventory approving material risk exposure and fulfilling regulatory requirement market risk that impact business outside of global market are monitored and governed by their respective governance function model risk is the potential for adverse consequence from decision based on incorrect or misused model output and report given that model are used across the corporation model risk impact all risk type including credit market and operational risk the enterprise model risk policy defines model risk standard consistent with our risk framework and risk appetite prevailing regulatory guidance and industry best practice all model including risk management valuation and regulatory capital model must meet certain validation criterion including effective challenge of the conceptual soundness of the model independent model testing and ongoing monitoring through outcome analysis and benchmarking the enterprise model risk committee subcommittee of the mrc oversees that model standard are consistent with model risk requirement and monitor the effective challenge in the model validation process across the corporation interest rate riskinterest rate risk represents exposure to instrument whose value vary with the level or volatility of interest rate these instrument include but are not limited to loan debt security certain trading related asset and liability deposit borrowing and derivative hedging instrument used to mitigate these risk include derivative such option future forward and swap foreign exchange riskforeign exchange risk represents exposure to change in the value of current holding and future cash flow denominated in currency other than the dollar the type of instrument exposed to this risk include investment in non subsidiary foreign currency denominated loan and security future cash flow in foreign currency arising from foreign exchange transaction foreign currency denominated debt and various foreign exchange derivative whose value fluctuate with change in the level or volatility of currency exchange rate or non interest rate hedging instrument used to mitigate this risk include foreign exchange option currency swap future forward and foreign currency denominated debt and deposit mortgage riskmortgage risk represents exposure to change in the value of mortgage related instrument the value of these instrument are sensitive to prepayment rate mortgage rate agency debt rating default market liquidity government participation and interest rate volatility our exposure to these instrument take several form for example we trade and engage in market making activity in variety of mortgage security including whole loan pas through certificate commercial mortgage and collateralized mortgage obligation including collateralized debt obligation using mortgage underlying collateral in addition we originate variety of mb which involves the accumulation of mortgage related loan in anticipation of eventual securitization and we may hold position in mortgage security and residential mortgage loan part of the alm portfolio we also record msrs part of our mortgage origination activity hedging instrument used to mitigate this risk include derivative such option swap future and forward well security including mb and treasury security for more information see mortgage banking risk management on page equity market riskequity market risk represents exposure to security that represent an ownership interest in corporation in the form of domestic and foreign common stock or other equity linked instrument instrument that would lead to this exposure include but are not limited to the following common stock exchange traded fund american depositary receipt convertible bond listed equity option put and call otc equity option equity total return swap equity index future and other equity derivative product hedging instrument used to mitigate this risk include option future swap convertible bond and cash position commodity riskcommodity risk represents exposure to instrument traded in the petroleum natural gas power and metal market these instrument consist primarily of future forward swap and option hedging instrument used to mitigate this risk include option future and swap in the same or similar commodity product well cash position bank of americaissuer credit riskissuer credit risk represents exposure to change in the creditworthiness of individual issuer or group of issuer our portfolio is exposed to issuer credit risk where the value of an asset may be adversely impacted by change in the level of credit spread by credit migration or by default hedging instrument used to mitigate this risk include bond cd and other credit fixed income instrument market liquidity riskmarket liquidity risk represents the risk that the level of expected market activity change dramatically and in certain case may even cease this expose to the risk that we will not be able to transact business and execute trade in an orderly manner which may impact our result this impact could be further exacerbated if expected hedging or pricing correlation are compromised by disproportionate demand or lack of demand for certain instrument we utilize various risk mitigating technique discussed in more detail in trading risk management trading risk managementto evaluate risk in our trading activity we focus on the actual and potential volatility of revenue generated by individual position well portfolio of position various technique and procedure are utilized to enable the most complete understanding of these risk quantitative measure of market risk are evaluated on daily basis from single position to the portfolio of the corporation these measure include sensitivity of position to various market risk factor such the potential impact on revenue from one basis point change in interest rate and statistical measure utilizing both actual and hypothetical market move such var and stress testing period of extreme market stress influence the reliability of these technique to varying degree qualitative evaluation of market risk utilize the suite of quantitative risk measure while understanding each of their respective limitation additionally risk manager independently evaluate the risk of the portfolio under the current market environment and potential future environment var is common statistic used to measure market risk it allows the aggregation of market risk factor including the effect of portfolio diversification var model simulates the value of portfolio under range of scenario in order to generate distribution of potential gain and loss var represents the loss portfolio is not expected to exceed more than certain number of time per period based on specified holding period confidence level and window of historical data we use one var model consistently across the trading portfolio and it us historical simulation approach based on three year window of historical data our primary var statistic is equivalent to percent confidence level which mean that for var with one day holding period there should not be loss in excess of var on average out of trading day within any var model there are significant and numerous assumption that will differ from company to company the accuracy of var model depends on the availability and quality of historical data for each of the risk factor in the portfolio var model may require additional modeling assumption for new product that do not have the necessary historical market data or for le liquid position for which accurate daily price are not consistently available for position with insufficient historical data for the var calculation the process for establishing an appropriate proxy is based on fundamental and statistical analysis of the new product or le liquid position this analysis identifies reasonable alternative that replicate both the expected volatility and correlation to other market risk factor that the missing data would be expected to experience var may not be indicative of realized revenue volatility change in market condition or in the composition of the portfolio can have material impact on the result in particular the historical data used for the var calculation might indicate higher or lower level of portfolio diversification than will be experienced in order for the var model to reflect current market condition we update the historical data underlying our var model on weekly basis or more frequently during period of market stress and regularly review the assumption underlying the model minor portion of risk related to our trading position is not included in var these risk are reviewed part of our icaap for more information regarding icaap see capital management on page grm continually review evaluates and enhances our var model so that it reflects the material risk in our trading portfolio change to the var model are reviewed and approved prior to implementation and any material change are reported to management through the appropriate management committee trading limit on quantitative risk measure including var are independently set by global market risk management and reviewed on regular basis so that trading limit remain relevant and within our overall risk appetite for market risk trading limit are reviewed in the context of market liquidity volatility and strategic business priority trading limit are set at both granular level to allow for extensive coverage of risk well at aggregated portfolio to account for correlation among risk factor all trading limit are approved at least annually approved trading limit are stored and tracked in centralized limit management system trading limit excess are communicated to management for review certain quantitative market risk measure and corresponding limit have been identified critical in the corporation risk appetite statement these risk appetite limit are reported on daily basis and are approved at least annually by the erc and the board in period of market stress global market senior leadership communicates daily to discus loss key risk position and any limit excess result of this process the business may selectively reduce risk table present the total market based portfolio var which is the combination of the total covered position and le liquid trading position portfolio and the fair value option portfolio covered position are defined by regulatory standard trading asset and liability both on and off balance sheet that meet defined set of specification these specification identify the most liquid trading position which are intended to be held for short term horizon and where we are able to hedge the material risk element in two way market position in le liquid market or where there are restriction on the ability to trade the position typically do not qualify covered position foreign exchange and commodity position are always considered covered position except for structural foreign currency position that are excluded with prior regulatory approval in addition table present our fair value option portfolio which includes substantially all of the funded and unfunded exposure for which we elect the fair value option and their corresponding hedge additionally market risk var for trading activity presented in table differs from var used for regulatory capital calculation due to the holding period being bank of america the holding period for var used for regulatory capital calculation is day while for the market risk var presented below fair value option portfolio diversification total market based portfolio backtestingthe accuracy of the var methodology is evaluated by backtesting which compare the daily var result utilizing one day holding period against comparable subset of trading revenue backtesting excess occurs when trading loss exceeds the var for the corresponding day these excess are evaluated to understand the position and market move that produced the trading loss with goal to help confirm that the var methodology accurately represents those loss we expect the frequency of trading loss in excess of var to be in line with the confidence level of the var statistic being tested for example with percent confidence level we expect one trading loss in excess of var every day or between two to three trading loss in excess of var over the course of year the number of backtesting excess observed can differ from the statistically expected number of excess if the current level of market volatility is materially different than the level of market volatility that existed during the three year of historical data used in the var calculation the trading revenue used for backtesting is defined by regulatory agency in order to most closely align with the var component of the regulatory capital calculation this revenue differs from total trading related revenue in that it excludes revenue from trading activity that either do not generate market risk or the market risk can not be included in var some example of the type of revenue excluded for backtesting are fee commission reserve net interest income and intra day trading revenue we conduct daily backtesting on the var result used for regulatory capital calculation well the var result for key legal entity region and risk factor these result are reported to senior market risk management senior management regularly review and evaluates the result of these test during there wa one day where this subset of trading revenue had loss that exceeded our total covered portfolio var utilizing one day holding period total trading related revenuetotal trading related revenue excluding brokerage fee and cva dva and funding valuation adjustment gain million trading portfolio stress testingbecause the nature of var model suggests result can exceed our estimate and it is dependent on limited historical window we also stress test our portfolio using scenario analysis this analysis estimate the change in the value of our trading portfolio that may result from abnormal market movement set of scenario categorized either historical or hypothetical are computed daily for the overall trading portfolio and individual business these scenario include shock to underlying market risk factor that may be well beyond the shock found in the historical data used to calculate var bank of america scenario simulate the impact of the market move that occurred during period of extended historical market stress generally multi week period representing the most severe point during crisis is selected for each historical scenario hypothetical scenario provide estimated portfolio impact from potential future market stress event scenario are reviewed and updated in response to changing position and new economic or political information in addition new or ad hoc scenario are developed to address specific potential market event or particular vulnerability in the portfolio the stress test are reviewed on regular basis and the result are presented to senior management stress testing for the trading portfolio is integrated with enterprise wide stress testing and incorporated into the limit framework the macroeconomic scenario used for enterprise wide stress testing purpose differ from the typical trading portfolio scenario in that they have longer time horizon and the result are forecasted over multiple period for use in consolidated capital and liquidity planning for more information see managing risk on page interest rate risk management for the banking bookthe following discussion present net interest income for banking book activity interest rate risk represents the most significant market risk exposure to our banking book balance sheet interest rate risk is measured the potential change in net interest income caused by movement in market interest rate client facing activity primarily lending and deposit taking create interest rate sensitive position on our balance sheet we prepare forward looking forecast of net interest income the baseline forecast take into consideration expected future business growth alm positioning and the future direction of interest rate movement implied by market based forward curve we measure and evaluate the impact that alternative interest rate scenario have on the baseline forecast in order to ass interest rate sensitivity under varied condition the net interest income forecast is frequently updated for changing assumption and differing outlook based on economic trend market condition and business strategy thus we continually monitor our banking book balance sheet position in order to maintain an acceptable level of exposure to interest rate change the interest rate scenario that we analyze incorporate balance sheet assumption such loan and deposit growth and pricing change in funding mix product repricing maturity characteristic and investment security premium amortization our overall goal is to manage interest rate risk so that movement in interest rate do not significantly adversely affect earnings and capital table present the spot and month forward rate used in developing the forward curve used in our baseline forecast at december and table ratesdecember federalfundsthree yearswapspot month forward december month forward table show the pretax impact to forecasted net interest income over the next month from december and resulting from instantaneous parallel and non parallel shock to the market based forward curve periodically we evaluate the scenario presented so that they are meaningful in the context of the current rate environment the interest rate scenario also assume dollar interest rate are floored at zero depending on the level of interest rate down rate scenario may not receive the full impact of the rate shock particularly in low rate environment the overall decrease in asset sensitivity shown in the following table to up rate scenario wa primarily due to an increase in long end and short end rate we continue to be asset sensitive to parallel upward move in interest rate with the majority of that impact coming from the short end of the yield curve additionally higher interest rate negatively impact the fair value of our debt security classified available for sale and adversely affect accumulated oci and thus capital level under the basel capital rule under instantaneous upward parallel shift the near term adverse impact to basel capital would be reduced over time by offsetting positive impact to interest rate and foreign exchange derivative contractswe use interest rate and foreign exchange derivative contract in our alm activity to manage our interest rate and foreign exchange risk specifically we use those derivative to manage both the variability in cash flow and change in fair value of various asset and liability arising from those risk our interest rate derivative contract are generally non leveraged swap tied to various benchmark interest rate and foreign exchange basis swap option future and forward and our foreign exchange contract include cross currency interest rate swap foreign currency future contract foreign currency forward contract and option the derivative used in our alm activity can be split into two broad category designated accounting hedge and other risk management derivative designated accounting hedge are primarily used to manage our exposure to interest rate described in the interest rate risk management for the banking book section and are included in the sensitivity presented in table the corporation also us foreign currency derivative in accounting hedge to manage substantially all of the foreign exchange risk of our foreign operation by hedging the foreign exchange risk of our foreign operation the corporation market risk exposure in this area is not significant risk management derivative are predominantly used to hedge foreign exchange risk related to various foreign currency denominated asset and liability and eliminate substantially all foreign currency exposure in the cash flow of the corporation non trading foreign currency denominated financial instrument these foreign exchange derivative are sensitive to other market risk exposure such cross currency basis spread and interest rate risk however these feature are not significant component of these foreign exchange derivative the market risk related to this exposure is not significant for more information on the accounting for derivative see note managementcompliance risk is the risk of legal or regulatory sanction material financial loss or damage to the reputation of the corporation arising from the failure of the corporation to comply with the requirement of applicable law rule regulation and our internal policy and procedure collectively applicable law rule and regulation we are subject to comprehensive regulation under federal and state law rule and regulation in the and the law of the various jurisdiction in which we operate including those related to financial crime and anti money laundering market conduct trading activity fair lending privacy data protection and unfair deceptive or abusive act or practice operational risk is the risk of loss resulting from inadequate or failed process or system people or external event and includes legal risk operational risk may occur anywhere in the corporation including third party business process and is not limited to operation function the corporation face number of key operational risk including third party risk model risk conduct risk technology risk information security risk and data risk operational risk can result in financial loss and reputational impact and is component in the calculation of total rwa used in the basel capital calculation for more information on basel calculation see capital management on page flu and control function are first and foremost responsible for managing all aspect of their business including their compliance and operational risk flu and control function are required to understand their business process and related risk and control including third party dependency and the related regulatory requirement and monitor and report on the effectiveness of the control environment in order to actively monitor and ass the performance of their process and control they must conduct comprehensive quality assurance activity and identify issue and risk to remediate control gap and weakness flu and control function must also adhere to compliance and operational risk appetite limit to meet strategic capital and financial planning objective finally flu and control function are responsible for the proactive identification management and escalation of compliance and operational risk across the corporation collectively these effort are important to strengthen their compliance and operational resiliency which is the ability to deliver critical operation through disruption global compliance and operational risk team independently ass compliance and operational risk monitor business activity and process and evaluate flu and control function for adherence to applicable law rule and regulation including identifying issue and risk and reporting bank of america the state of the control environment corporate audit provides an independent assessment and validation through testing of key compliance and operational risk process and control across the corporation the corporation global compliance enterprise policy and operational risk management enterprise policy set the requirement for reporting compliance and operational risk information to executive management well the board or appropriate board level committee and reflect global compliance and operational risk responsibility for conducting independent oversight of the corporation compliance and operational risk management activity the board provides oversight of compliance risk through it audit committee and the erc and operational risk through it erc key operational risk facing the corporation is information security which includes cybersecurity cybersecurity risk includes exposure to failure or interruption of service or security breach resulting from malicious technological attack that impact the confidentiality integrity or availability of our or third party operation system or data the corporation seek to mitigate information security risk and associated reputational and compliance risk by employing multi layered and intelligence led global information security program focused on preparing for preventing detecting mitigating responding to and recovering from cyber threat and incident and effectively operating the corporation process additionally our business continuity policy standard and procedure are designed to maintain the availability of business function and enable impacted unit within the corporation and third party to achieve strategic objective in the event of cybersecurity incident the global information security program is supported by three line of defense the global information security team within the first line of defense is responsible for the day to day management of the global information security program which includes defining policy and procedure to safeguard the corporation information system and data conducting vulnerability and third party information security assessment information security event management responding to ransomware and distributed denial of service attack evaluation of external cyber intelligence supporting industry cybersecurity effort and working with governmental agency and developing employee training to support adherence to the corporation policy and procedure the second line of defense global compliance and operational risk independently ass monitor and test information security risk across the corporation well the effectiveness of the global information security program corporate audit serf the third line of defense conducting additional independent review and validation of the first line process and function part of our global information security program we leverage both internal and external assessment and partnership with industry leader to help approach information security holistically additionally the corporation maintains comprehensive enterprise wide program that defines standard for the planning sourcing management and oversight of third party relationship and third party access to it system facility and or confidential or proprietary data for business purpose or supervisory function through established governance structure we have process to help facilitate appropriate and effective oversight of information security risk these routine enable our three line of defense and management to debate information security risk and monitor control performance to allow for further escalation to executive management management and board level committee or to the board appropriate the board is actively engaged in the oversight of bank of america global information security program and devotes significant time and attention to the oversight of cybersecurity and information security risk the board regularly discus cybersecurity and information security risk with the chief technology and information officer and the chief information security officer additionally the erc receives regular reporting and review and approves the information security program and policy on an annual basis reputational risk managementreputational risk is the risk that negative perception of the corporation may adversely impact profitability or operation reputational risk may result from many of the corporation activity including those related to the management of our strategic operational compliance and credit risk the corporation manages reputational risk through established policy and control embedded throughout it business and risk management process we proactively monitor and identify potential reputational risk event and have process established to mitigate reputational risk in timely manner if reputational risk event occur we focus on remediating the underlying issue and taking action to minimize damage to the corporation reputation the corporation ha process and procedure in place to respond to event that give rise to reputational risk including educating individual and organization that influence public opinion implementing external communication strategy to mitigate the risk and informing key stakeholder of potential reputational risk the corporation organization and governance structure provides oversight of reputational risk reputational risk reporting is provided regularly and directly to senior management and the erc which provides primary oversight of reputational risk in addition each flu ha committee which includes representative from legal and risk that is responsible for the oversight of reputational risk including approval for business activity that present elevated level of reputational risk climate risk managementclimate related risk are divided into two major category risk related to the physical impact of climate change driven by extreme weather event such hurricane and flood well chronic longer term shift such rising average global temperature and sea level and risk related to the transition to low carbon economy which may entail extensive policy legal technology and market change these change and event may have broad impact on operation supply chain distribution network customer and market and are otherwise referred to respectively physical risk and transition risk these risk may impact both financial and nonfinancial risk type physical risk may lead to increased credit risk by diminishing borrower repayment capacity or impacting the value of collateral physical risk may also increase operational risk by impacting the corporation facility employee customer or vendor transition risk may amplify credit risk through the financial impact of change in policy technology or the market on the corporation or it counterparties unanticipated market change can lead to sudden price adjustment and give rise to heightened market risk in addition reputational risk may arise including from our climate related practice and disclosure and if we do not meet our climate related commitment effective management of climate risk requires coordinated governance clearly defined role and responsibility and well bank of americadeveloped process to identify measure monitor and control risk climate risk span all key risk type we have developed and continue to enhance process to embed climate risk consideration into our risk framework and risk management program established for strategic credit market liquidity compliance operational and reputational risk our environmental and social risk policy framework aligns with our risk framework and provides additional clarity and transparency regarding our approach to environmental and social risk inclusive of climate risk our governance framework establishes oversight of climate risk practice and strategy by the board supported by it erc well the mrc and the responsible growth committee both of which are management level committee comprised of senior leader across every major flu and control function the responsible growth committee is supported by the esg disclosure sub committee which is responsible for reviewing and providing oversight of the corporation climate and esg related public disclosure our climate risk management effort are overseen by an executive officer who report to the cro the climate risk council which consists of leader across risk flu and control function meet routinely to discus our approach to managing climate related risk in line with our risk framework in we publicly announced our commitment to achieve net zero emission in our financing activity operation and supply chain before net zero goal and set emission target for our operation and supply chain in connection with our net zero goal in we announced target to reduce emission by associated with our financing activity related to auto manufacturing energy and power generation target in our september task force on climate related financial disclosure report we disclosed our and financed emission and emission intensity metric for these sector with serving the baseline for our target we plan to disclose the financed emission for additional portion of our business loan portfolio in and we plan to set financing activity emission reduction target for other key sector by april achieving our climate related goal and target including our net zero goal and target may require technological advance clearly defined roadmaps for industry sector new standard and public policy including those that improve the cost of capital for the transition to low carbon economy and better emission data reporting well ongoing strong and active engagement with customer supplier investor government official and other stakeholder given the extended period of these and other climate related goal we have established our initiative have not resulted in significant effect on our result of operation or financial position in the relevant period presented herein for outstanding loan and lease and allowance for credit loss to the consolidated financial statement the determination of the allowance for credit loss is based on numerous estimate and assumption which require bank of america high degree of judgment and are often interrelated critical judgment in the process is the weighting of our forward looking macroeconomic scenario that are incorporated into our quantitative model any one economic outlook is inherently uncertain the corporation us multiple macroeconomic scenario in it ecl calculation which have included baseline scenario derived from consensus estimate an adverse scenario reflecting an extended moderate recession downside scenario reflecting persistent inflation and interest rate above the baseline scenario tail risk scenario similar to the severely adverse scenario used in stress testing and an upside scenario that considers the potential for improvement above the baseline scenario the overall economic outlook is weighted percent towards recessionary environment in with continued inflationary pressure leading to lower gross domestic product gdp and higher unemployment rate expectation compared to the prior year generally the consensus estimate improve or deteriorate the allowance for credit loss will change in similar direction there are multiple variable that drive the macroeconomic scenario with the key variable including but not limited to gdp and unemployment rate of december the weighted macroeconomic outlook for the average unemployment rate wa forecasted at percent percent and percent in the fourth quarter of and respectively and the weighted macroeconomic outlook for gdp wa forecasted to grow at percent percent and percent year over year in the fourth quarter of and respectively of december the latest consensus estimate for the average unemployment rate for the fourth quarter of wa percent and gdp wa forecasted to grow percent year over year in the fourth quarter of reflecting tighter labor market and depressed growth expectation compared to our macroeconomic outlook of december and were factored into our allowance for credit loss estimate of december in addition of december the weighted macroeconomic outlook for the average unemployment rate wa forecasted at percent and percent in the fourth quarter of and and the weighted macroeconomic outlook for gdp wa forecasted to contract percent and grow percent year over year in the fourth quarter of and in addition to the above judgment and estimate the allowance for credit loss can also be impacted by unanticipated change in asset quality of the portfolio such increase or decrease in credit and or internal risk rating in our commercial portfolio improvement or deterioration in borrower delinquency or credit score in our credit card portfolio and increase or decrease in home price which is primary driver of ltvs in our consumer real estate portfolio all of which have some degree of uncertainty macroeconomic scenario and other assumption on the estimate of our allowance for credit loss the corporation compared the december modeled ecl from the baseline scenario and our adverse scenario relative to the baseline scenario the adverse scenario assumed peak unemployment rate of nearly three percentage point higher than the baseline scenario decline in gdp followed by prolonged recovery and lower home price outlook with difference of approximately eight percent at the trough this sensitivity analysis resulted in hypothetical increase in the allowance for credit loss of approximately billion while the sensitivity analysis may be useful to understand how change in macroeconomic assumption could impact our modeled ecls it is not meant to forecast how our allowance for credit loss is expected to change in different macroeconomic outlook importantly the analysis doe not incorporate variety of factor including qualitative reserve and the weighting of alternate scenario which could have offsetting effect on the estimate considering the variety of factor contemplated when developing and weighting macroeconomic outlook such recent economic event leading economic indicator view of internal and third party economist and industry trend in addition to other qualitative factor the corporation belief the allowance for credit loss at december is appropriate fair value of financial internal control over financial reporting the management of bank of america corporation is responsible for establishing and maintaining adequate internal control over financial reporting the corporation internal control over financial reporting is process designed to provide reasonable assurance regarding the reliability of financial reporting and the preparation of financial statement for external purpose in accordance with accounting principle generally accepted in the united state of america the corporation internal control over financial reporting includes those policy and procedure that pertain to the maintenance of record that in reasonable detail accurately and fairly reflect the transaction and disposition of the asset of the corporation ii provide reasonable assurance that transaction are recorded necessary to permit preparation of financial statement in accordance with accounting principle generally accepted in the united state of america and that receipt and expenditure of the corporation are being made only in accordance with authorization of management and director of the corporation and iii provide reasonable assurance regarding prevention or timely detection of unauthorized acquisition use or disposition of the corporation asset that could have material effect on the financial statement because of it inherent limitation internal control over financial reporting may not prevent or detect misstatement also projection of any evaluation of effectiveness to future period are subject to the risk that control may become inadequate because of change in condition or that the degree of compliance with the policy or procedure may deteriorate management assessed the effectiveness of the corporation internal control over financial reporting of december based on the framework set forth by the committee of sponsoring organization of the treadway commission in internal control integrated framework based on that assessment management concluded that of december the corporation internal control over financial reporting is effective the corporation internal control over financial reporting of december ha been audited by
