note to consolidated financial statement bank of americabank of america corporation and subsidiariesnotes to consolidated financial statementsnote summary of significant accounting principlesbank of america corporation bank holding company and financial holding company provides diverse range of financial service and product throughout the and in certain international market the term the corporation used herein may refer to bank of america corporation individually bank of america corporation and it subsidiary or certain of bank of america corporation subsidiary or affiliate principle of consolidation and basis of presentationthe consolidated financial statement include the account of the corporation and it majority owned subsidiary and those variable interest entity vies where the corporation is the primary beneficiary intercompany account and transaction have been eliminated result of operation of acquired company are included from the date of acquisition and for vies from the date that the corporation became the primary beneficiary asset held in an agency or fiduciary capacity are not included in the consolidated financial statement the corporation account for investment in company for which it owns voting interest and for which it ha the ability to exercise significant influence over operating and financing decision using the equity method of accounting these investment which include the corporation interest in affordable housing and renewable energy partnership are recorded in other asset equity method investment are subject to impairment testing and the corporation proportionate share of income or loss is included in other income the preparation of the consolidated financial statement in conformity with accounting principle generally accepted in the united state of america requires management to make estimate and assumption that affect reported amount and disclosure actual result could materially differ from those estimate and assumption certain prior period amount have been reclassified to conform to current period presentation new accounting standardshedge accounting the fasb issued new accounting standard that make targeted improvement to the application of the fair value hedge accounting guidance for closed portfolio of financial asset the targeted improvement were effective january on prospective basis financial instrument credit lossesthe fasb amended the accounting and disclosure requirement for expected credit loss ecl by removing the recognition and measurement guidance on troubled debt restructurings tdrs and adding disclosure on the financial effect and subsequent performance of certain type of modification made to borrower experiencing financial difficulty the effect of these change on the corporation consolidated financial position result of operation or disclosure in the note to the consolidated financial statement are not significant the amendment were effective on january which the corporation adopted using modified retrospective approach significant accounting principlescash and cash equivalentscash and cash equivalent include cash on hand cash item in the process of collection cash segregated under federal and other brokerage regulation and amount due from correspondent bank the federal reserve bank and certain non central bank certain cash balance are restricted to withdrawal or usage by legally binding contractual agreement or regulatory requirement security financing agreementssecurities borrowed or purchased under agreement to resell and security loaned or sold under agreement to repurchase security financing agreement are treated collateralized financing transaction except in instance where the transaction is required to be accounted for individual sale and purchase transaction generally these agreement are recorded at acquisition or sale price plus accrued interest in instance where the interest is negative the corporation policy is to present negative interest on financial asset interest income and negative interest on financial liability interest expense for security financing agreement that are accounted for under the fair value option the change in the fair value of these security financing agreement are recorded in market making and similar activity in the consolidated statement of income the corporation policy is to monitor the market value of the principal amount loaned under resale agreement and obtain collateral from or return collateral pledged to counterparties when appropriate security financing agreement do not create material credit risk due to these collateral provision therefore an allowance for loan loss is not necessary in transaction where the corporation act the lender in security lending agreement and receives security that can be pledged or sold collateral it recognizes an asset on the consolidated balance sheet at fair value representing the security received and liability representing the obligation to return those security trading instrumentsfinancial instrument utilized in trading activity are carried at fair value fair value is generally based on quoted market price for the same or similar asset and liability if these market price are not available fair value are estimated based on dealer quote pricing model discounted cash flow methodology or similar technique where the determination of fair value may require significant management judgment or estimation realized gain and loss are recorded on trade date basis realized and unrealized gain and loss are recognized in market making and similar activity derivative and hedging activitiesderivatives are entered into on behalf of customer for trading or to support risk management activity derivative used in risk management activity include derivative that are both designated in qualifying accounting hedge relationship and derivative used to hedge market risk in relationship that are not designated in qualifying accounting hedge relationship referred to other risk management activity the corporation manages interest rate and foreign currency exchange rate sensitivity predominantly through the use of derivative derivative utilized by the corporation include swap future and forward settlement contract and option contract bank of america derivative are recorded on the consolidated balance sheet at fair value taking into consideration the effect of legally enforceable master netting agreement that allow the corporation to settle positive and negative position and offset cash collateral held with the same counterparty on net basis for exchange traded contract fair value is based on quoted market price in active or inactive market or is derived from observable market based pricing parameter similar to those applied to over the counter otc derivative for non exchange traded contract fair value is based on dealer quote pricing model discounted cash flow methodology or similar technique for which the determination of fair value may require significant management judgment or estimation valuation of derivative asset and liability reflect the value of the instrument including counterparty credit risk these value also take into account the corporation own credit standing trading derivative and other risk management activitiesderivatives held for trading purpose are included in derivative asset or derivative liability on the consolidated balance sheet with change in fair value included in market making and similar activity derivative used for other risk management activity are included in derivative asset or derivative liability derivative used in other risk management activity have not been designated in qualifying accounting hedge relationship because they did not qualify or the risk that is being mitigated pertains to an item that is reported at fair value through earnings so that the effect of measuring the derivative instrument and the asset or liability to which the risk exposure pertains will offset in the consolidated statement of income to the extent effective the change in the fair value of derivative that serve to mitigate certain risk associated with mortgage servicing right msrs interest rate lock commitment irlcs and first lien mortgage loan held for sale lhfs that are originated by the corporation are recorded in other income change in the fair value of derivative that serve to mitigate interest rate risk and foreign currency risk are included in market making and similar activity credit derivative are also used by the corporation to mitigate the risk associated with various credit exposure the change in the fair value of these derivative are included in market making and similar activity and other income derivative used for hedge accounting purpose accounting hedge for accounting hedge the corporation formally document at inception all relationship between hedging instrument and hedged item well the risk management objective and strategy for undertaking various accounting hedge additionally the corporation primarily us regression analysis at the inception of hedge and for each reporting period thereafter to ass whether the derivative used in an accounting hedge transaction is expected to be and ha been highly effective in offsetting change in the fair value or cash flow of hedged item or forecasted transaction the corporation discontinues hedge accounting when it is determined that derivative is not expected to be or ha ceased to be highly effective hedge and then reflects change in fair value of the derivative in earnings after termination of the hedge relationship fair value hedge are used to protect against change in the fair value of the corporation asset and liability that are attributable to interest rate or foreign exchange volatility change in the fair value of derivative designated fair value hedge are recorded in earnings together and in the same income statement line item with change in the fair value of the related hedged item if derivative instrument in fair value hedge is terminated or the hedge designation removed the previous adjustment to the carrying value of the hedged asset or liability are subsequently accounted for in the same manner other component of the carrying value of that asset or liability for interest earning asset and interest bearing liability such adjustment are amortized to earnings over the remaining life of the respective asset or liability cash flow hedge are used primarily to minimize the variability in cash flow of asset and liability or forecasted transaction caused by interest rate or foreign exchange rate fluctuation the corporation also us cash flow hedge to hedge the price risk associated with deferred compensation change in the fair value of derivative used in cash flow hedge are recorded in accumulated other comprehensive income oci and are reclassified into the line item in the income statement in which the hedged item is recorded in the same period the hedged item affect earnings component of derivative that are excluded in assessing hedge effectiveness are recorded in the same income statement line item the hedged item net investment hedge are used to manage the foreign exchange rate sensitivity arising from net investment in foreign operation change in the spot price of derivative that are designated net investment hedge of foreign operation are recorded component of accumulated oci the remaining component of these derivative are excluded in assessing hedge effectiveness and are recorded in market making and similar activity securitiesdebt security are reported on the consolidated balance sheet at their trade date their classification is dependent on the purpose for which the security were acquired debt security purchased for use in the corporation trading activity are reported in trading account asset at fair value with unrealized gain and loss included in market making and similar activity substantially all other debt security purchased are used in the corporation asset and liability management alm activity and are reported on the consolidated balance sheet either debt security carried at fair value or held to maturity htm debt security debt security carried at fair value are either available for sale afs security with unrealized gain and loss net of tax included in accumulated oci or carried at fair value with unrealized gain and loss reported in market making and similar activity htm debt security are debt security that management ha the intent and ability to hold to maturity and are reported at amortized cost the corporation evaluates each afs security where the value ha declined below amortized cost if the corporation intends to sell or belief it is more likely than not that it will be required to sell the debt security it is written down to fair value through earnings for afs debt security the corporation intends to hold the corporation evaluates the debt security for ecl except for debt security that are guaranteed by the treasury government agency or sovereign entity of high credit quality where the corporation applies zero credit loss assumption for the remaining afs debt security the corporation considers qualitative parameter such internal and external credit rating and the value of underlying collateral if an afs debt security fails any of the qualitative parameter discounted cash flow analysis is used by the corporation to bank of americadetermine if portion of the unrealized loss is result of an ecl the corporation will then recognize either credit loss expense or reversal of credit loss expense in other income for the amount necessary to adjust the debt security valuation allowance to it current estimate of expected credit loss cash flow expected to be collected are estimated using all relevant information available such remaining payment term prepayment speed the financial condition of the issuer expected default and the value of the underlying collateral if any of the decline in fair value is related to market factor that amount is recognized in accumulated oci in certain instance the credit loss may exceed the total decline in fair value in which case the allowance recorded is limited to the difference between the amortized cost and the fair value of the asset the corporation separately evaluates it htm debt security for any credit loss of which substantially all qualify for the zero loss assumption for the remaining security the corporation performs discounted cash flow analysis to estimate any credit loss which are then recognized part of the allowance for credit loss interest on debt security including amortization of premium and accretion of discount is included in interest income premium and discount are amortized or accreted to interest income at constant effective yield over the contractual life of the security realized gain and loss from the sale of debt security are determined using the specific identification method equity security with readily determinable fair value that are not held for trading purpose are carried at fair value with unrealized gain and loss included in other income equity security that do not have readily determinable fair value are recorded at cost le impairment if any plus or minus qualifying observable price change these security are reported in other asset loan and leasesloans with the exception of loan accounted for under the fair value option are measured at historical cost and reported at their outstanding principal balance net of any unearned income charge offs unamortized deferred fee and cost on originated loan and for purchased loan net of any unamortized premium or discount loan origination fee and certain direct origination cost are deferred and recognized adjustment to interest income over the life of the related loan unearned income discount and premium are amortized to interest income using level yield methodology the corporation elect to account for certain consumer and commercial loan under the fair value option with interest reported in interest income and change in fair value reported in market making and similar activity or other income under applicable accounting guidance for reporting purpose the loan and lease portfolio is categorized by portfolio segment and within each portfolio segment by class of financing receivable portfolio segment is defined the level at which an entity develops and document systematic methodology to determine the allowance for credit loss and class of financing receivable is defined the level of disaggregation of portfolio segment based on the initial measurement attribute risk characteristic and method for assessing risk the corporation three portfolio segment are consumer real estate credit card and other consumer and commercial the class within the consumer real estate portfolio segment are residential mortgage and home equity the class within the credit card and other consumer portfolio segment are credit card direct indirect consumer and other consumer the class within the commercial portfolio segment are commercial non commercial commercial real estate commercial lease financing and small business commercial leasesthe corporation provides equipment financing to it customer through variety of lessor arrangement direct financing lease and sale type lease are carried at the aggregate of lease payment receivable plus the estimated residual value of the leased property le unearned income which is accreted to interest income over the lease term using method that approximate the interest method operating lease income is recognized on straight line basis the corporation lease arrangement generally do not contain non lease component allowance for credit losseson january the corporation adopted the new accounting standard that requires the measurement of the allowance for credit loss which includes both the allowance for loan and lease loss and the reserve for unfunded lending commitment to be based on management best estimate of the ecl in the corporation loan and lease portfolio excluding loan and unfunded lending commitment accounted for under the fair value option upon adoption billion or percent increase in the allowance for credit loss wa recorded on january which wa comprised of net increase of billion in the allowance for loan and lease loss and million increase in the reserve for unfunded lending commitment the ecl on funded consumer and commercial loan and lease is referred to the allowance for loan and lease loss and is reported separately contra asset to loan and lease on the consolidated balance sheet the ecl for unfunded lending commitment including home equity line of credit helocs standby letter of credit sblcs and binding unfunded loan commitment is reported on the consolidated balance sheet in accrued expense and other liability the provision for credit loss related to the loan and lease portfolio and unfunded lending commitment is reported in the consolidated statement of income at the amount necessary to adjust the allowance for credit loss to the current estimate of ecl for loan and lease the ecl is typically estimated using quantitative method that consider variety of factor such historical loss experience the current credit quality of the portfolio well an economic outlook over the life of the loan the life of the loan for closed ended product is based on the contractual maturity of the loan adjusted for any expected prepayment the contractual maturity includes any extension option that are at the sole discretion of the borrower for open ended product line of credit the ecl is determined based on the maximum repayment term associated with future draw from credit line unless those line of credit are unconditionally cancellable credit card in which case the corporation doe not record any allowance in it loss forecasting framework the corporation incorporates forward looking information through the use of macroeconomic scenario applied over the forecasted life of the asset these macroeconomic scenario include variable that have historically been key driver of increase and decrease in credit loss these variable include but are not limited to unemployment rate real estate price gross domestic product level and corporate bond spread any one economic outlook is inherently uncertain the corporation leverage multiple scenario the scenario that are chosen each quarter bank of america the weighting given to each scenario depend on variety of factor including recent economic event leading economic indicator view of internal and third party economist and industry trend the estimate of credit loss includes expected recovery of amount previously charged off negative allowance if loan ha been charged off the expected cash flow on the loan are not limited by the current amortized cost balance instead expected cash flow can be assumed up to the unpaid principal balance immediately prior to the charge off the allowance for loan and lease loss for tdrs is measured based on the present value of projected future lifetime principal and interest cash flow discounted at the loan original effective interest rate or in case where foreclosure is probable or the loan is collateral dependent at the loan collateral value or it observable market price if available the measurement of ecl for the renegotiated consumer credit card tdr portfolio is based on the present value of projected cash flow discounted using the average tdr portfolio contractual interest rate excluding promotionally priced loan in effect prior to restructuring projected cash flow for tdrs use the same economic outlook discussed above for purpose of computing this specific loss component of the allowance larger impaired loan are evaluated individually and smaller impaired loan are evaluated pool also included in the allowance for loan and lease loss are qualitative reserve to cover loss that are expected but in the corporation assessment may not be adequately reflected in the quantitative method or the economic assumption described above for example factor that the corporation considers include change in lending policy and procedure business condition the nature and size of the portfolio portfolio concentration the volume and severity of past due loan and nonaccrual loan the effect of external factor such competition and legal and regulatory requirement among others further the corporation considers the inherent uncertainty in quantitative model that are built on historical data with the exception of the corporation credit card portfolio the corporation doe not include reserve for interest receivable in the measurement of the allowance for credit loss the corporation generally classifies consumer loan nonperforming at day past due and revers interest income for these loan at that time for credit card loan the corporation reserve for interest and fee part of the allowance for loan and lease loss upon charge off of credit card loan the corporation revers the interest and fee income against the income statement line item where it wa originally recorded the corporation ha identified the following three portfolio segment and measure the allowance for credit loss using the following method consumer real estateto estimate ecl for consumer loan secured by residential real estate the corporation estimate the number of loan that will default over the life of the existing portfolio after factoring in estimated prepayment using quantitative modeling methodology the attribute that are most significant in estimating the corporation ecl include refreshed loan to value ltv or in the case of subordinated lien refreshed combined ltv cltv borrower credit score month since origination and geography all of which are further broken down by present collection status whether the loan is current delinquent in default or in bankruptcy the estimate are based on the corporation historical experience with the loan portfolio adjusted to reflect the economic outlook the outlook on the unemployment rate and consumer real estate price are key factor that impact the frequency and severity of loss estimate the corporation doe not reserve for credit loss on the unpaid principal balance of loan insured by the federal housing administration fha and long term standby loan these loan are fully insured the corporation record reserve for unfunded lending commitment for the ecl associated with the undrawn portion of the corporation helocs which can only be canceled by the corporation if certain criterion are met the ecl associated with these unfunded lending commitment is calculated using the same model and methodology noted above and incorporate utilization assumption at time of default for loan that are more than day past due and collateral dependent tdrs the corporation base the allowance on the estimated fair value of the underlying collateral of the reporting date le cost to sell the fair value of the collateral securing these loan is generally determined using an automated valuation model avm that estimate the value of property by reference to market data including sale of comparable property and price trend specific to the metropolitan statistical area in which the property being valued is located in the event that an avm value is not available the corporation utilizes publicized index or if these method provide le reliable valuation the corporation us appraisal or broker price opinion to estimate the fair value of the collateral while there is inherent imprecision in these valuation the corporation belief that they are representative of this portfolio in the aggregate for loan that are more than day past due and collateral dependent tdrs with the exception of the corporation fully insured portfolio the outstanding balance of loan that is in excess of the estimated property value after adjusting for cost to sell is charged off if the estimated property value decrease in period subsequent to the initial charge off the corporation will record an additional charge off however if the value increase in period subsequent to the charge off the corporation will adjust the allowance to account for the increase but not to level above the cumulative charge off amount credit card and other consumercredit card are revolving line of credit without defined maturity date the estimated life of credit card receivable is determined by estimating the amount and timing of expected future payment borrower making full payment minimum payment or somewhere in between that it will take for receivable balance to pay off the ecl on the future payment incorporates the spending behavior of borrower through time using key borrower specific factor and the economic outlook described above the corporation applies all expected payment in accordance with the credit card accountability responsibility and disclosure act of paying down the highest interest rate bucket first then forecasted future payment are prioritized to pay off the oldest balance until it is brought to zero or an expected charge off amount unemployment rate outlook borrower credit score delinquency status and historical payment behavior are all key input into the credit card receivable loss forecasting model future draw on the credit card line are excluded from the ecl they are unconditionally cancellable the ecl for the consumer vehicle lending portfolio is also determined using quantitative method supplemented with bank of americaqualitative analysis the quantitative model estimate ecl giving consideration to key borrower and loan characteristic such delinquency status borrower credit score ltv ratio underlying collateral type and collateral value commercialthe ecl on commercial loan is forecasted using model that estimate credit loss over the loan contractual life at an individual loan level the model use the contractual term to forecast future principal cash flow while also considering expected prepayment for open ended commitment such revolving line of credit change in funded balance are captured by forecasting borrower draw and payment behavior over the remaining life of the commitment for loan collateralized with commercial real estate and for which the underlying asset is the primary source of repayment the loss forecasting model consider key loan and customer attribute such ltv ratio net operating income and debt service coverage and capture variation in behavior according to property type and region the outlook on the unemployment rate gross domestic product and forecasted real estate price are utilized to determine indicator such rent level and vacancy rate which impact the ecl estimate for all other commercial loan and lease the loss forecasting model determines the probability of transition to different credit risk rating or default at each point over the life of the asset based on the borrower current credit risk rating industry sector size of the exposure and the geographic market the severity of loss is determined based on the type of collateral securing the exposure the size of the exposure the borrower industry sector any guarantor and the geographic market assumption of expected loss are conditioned to the economic outlook and the model considers key economic variable such unemployment rate gross domestic product corporate bond spread real estate and other asset price and equity market return in addition to the allowance for loan and lease loss the corporation also estimate ecl related to unfunded lending commitment such letter of credit financial guarantee unfunded banker acceptance and binding loan commitment excluding commitment accounted for under the fair value option reserve are estimated for the unfunded exposure using the same model and methodology the funded exposure and are reported reserve for unfunded lending commitment nonperforming loan and lease charge offs and delinquenciesnonperforming loan and lease generally include loan and lease that have been placed on nonaccrual status loan accounted for under the fair value option and lhfs are not reported nonperforming when nonaccrual loan is deemed uncollectible it is charged off against the allowance for credit loss if the charged off amount is later recovered the amount is reversed through the allowance for credit loss at the recovery date charge offs are reported net of recovery net charge offs if recovery for the period are greater than charge offs net charge offs are reported negative amount in accordance with the corporation policy consumer real estate secured loan including residential mortgage and home equity loan are generally placed on nonaccrual status and classified nonperforming at day past due unless repayment of the loan is insured by the fha or through individually insured long term standby agreement with fannie mae fnma or freddie mac fhlmc the fully insured portfolio residential mortgage loan in the fully insured portfolio are not placed on nonaccrual status and therefore are not reported nonperforming junior lien home equity loan are placed on nonaccrual status and classified nonperforming when the underlying first lien mortgage loan becomes day past due even if the junior lien loan is current the outstanding balance of real estate secured loan that is in excess of the estimated property value le cost to sell is charged off no later than the end of the month in which the loan becomes day past due unless the loan is fully insured or for loan in bankruptcy within day of receipt of notification of filing with the remaining balance classified nonperforming credit card and other unsecured consumer loan are charged off when the loan becomes day past due within day after receipt of notification of death or bankruptcy or upon confirmation of fraud these loan continue to accrue interest until they are charged off and therefore are not reported nonperforming loan consumer vehicle loan are placed on nonaccrual status when they become day past due within day after receipt of notification of bankruptcy or death or upon confirmation of fraud these loan are charged off to their collateral value when the loan become day past due upon repossession of the collateral within day after receipt of notification of bankruptcy or death or upon confirmation of fraud if repossession of the collateral is not expected the loan are fully charged off commercial loan and lease excluding business card loan that are past due day or more to principal or interest or where reasonable doubt exists to timely collection including loan that are individually identified being impaired are generally placed on nonaccrual status and classified nonperforming unless well secured and in the process of collection business card loan are charged off in the same manner consumer credit card loan other commercial loan and lease are generally charged off when all or portion of the principal amount is determined to be uncollectible the entire balance of consumer loan or commercial loan or lease is contractually delinquent if the minimum payment is not received by the specified due date on the customer billing statement interest and fee continue to accrue on past due loan and lease until the date the loan is placed on nonaccrual status if applicable accrued interest receivable is reversed when loan and lease are placed on nonaccrual status interest collection on nonaccruing loan and lease for which the ultimate collectability of principal is uncertain are applied principal reduction otherwise such collection are credited to income when received loan and lease may be restored to accrual status when all principal and interest is current and full repayment of the remaining contractual principal and interest is expected troubled debt restructuringsconsumer and commercial loan and lease whose contractual term have been restructured in manner that grant concession to borrower experiencing financial difficulty are classified tdrs concession could include reduction in the interest rate to rate that is below market on the loan payment extension forgiveness of principal forbearance or other action designed to maximize collection loan that are carried at fair value and lhfs are not classified tdrs loan and lease whose contractual term have been modified in tdr and are current at the time of restructuring may remain on accrual status if there is demonstrated performance prior to the restructuring and payment in full under the restructured term is expected otherwise the loan are bank of america on nonaccrual status and reported nonperforming except for fully insured consumer real estate loan until there is sustained repayment performance for reasonable period generally six month if accruing tdrs cease to perform in accordance with their modified contractual term they are placed on nonaccrual status and reported nonperforming tdrs secured consumer loan that have been discharged in chapter bankruptcy and have not been reaffirmed by the borrower are classified tdrs at the time of discharge such loan are placed on nonaccrual status and written down to the estimated collateral value le cost to sell no later than at the time of discharge if these loan are contractually current interest collection are generally recorded in interest income on cash basis consumer real estate secured loan for which binding offer to restructure ha been extended are also classified tdrs credit card and other unsecured consumer loan that have been renegotiated in tdr generally remain on accrual status until the loan is either paid in full or charged off which occurs no later than the end of the month in which the loan becomes day past due or for loan that have been placed on fixed payment plan day past due loan that had previously been modified in tdr and is subsequently refinanced under current underwriting standard at market rate with no concessionary term is accounted for new loan and is no longer reported tdr loan held for saleloans that the corporation intends to sell in the foreseeable future including residential mortgage loan syndication and to lesser degree commercial real estate consumer finance and other loan are reported lhfs and are carried at the lower of aggregate cost or fair value the corporation account for certain lhfs including residential mortgage lhfs under the fair value option loan origination cost for lhfs carried at the lower of cost or fair value are capitalized part of the carrying value of the loan and upon the sale of loan are recognized part of the gain or loss in noninterest income lhfs that are on nonaccrual status and are reported nonperforming defined in the policy herein are reported separately from nonperforming loan and lease premise and equipmentpremises and equipment are carried at cost le accumulated depreciation and amortization depreciation and amortization are recognized using the straight line method over the estimated useful life of the asset estimated life range up to year for building up to year for furniture and equipment and the shorter of lease term or estimated useful life for leasehold improvement other assetsfor the corporation financial asset that are measured at amortized cost and are not included in debt security or loan and lease on the consolidated balance sheet the corporation evaluates these asset for ecl using various technique for asset that are subject to collateral maintenance provision including federal fund sold and security borrowed or purchased under agreement to resell where the collateral consists of daily margining of liquid and marketable asset where the margining is expected to be maintained into the foreseeable future the expected loss are assumed to be zero for all other asset the corporation performs qualitative analysis including consideration of historical loss and current economic condition to estimate any ecl which are then included in valuation account that is recorded contra asset against the amortized cost basis of the financial asset lessee arrangementssubstantially all of the corporation lessee arrangement are operating lease under these arrangement the corporation record right of use asset and lease liability at lease commencement right of use asset are reported in other asset on the consolidated balance sheet and the related lease liability are reported in accrued expense and other liability all lease are recorded on the consolidated balance sheet except lease with an initial term le than month for which the corporation made the short term lease election lease expense is recognized on straight line basis over the lease term and is recorded in occupancy and equipment expense in the consolidated statement of income the corporation made an accounting policy election not to separate lease and non lease component of contract that is or contains lease for it real estate and equipment lease such lease payment represent payment on both lease and non lease component at lease commencement lease liability are recognized based on the present value of the remaining lease payment and discounted using the corporation incremental borrowing rate right of use asset initially equal the lease liability adjusted for any lease payment made prior to lease commencement and for any lease incentive goodwill and intangible assetsgoodwill is the purchase premium after adjusting for the fair value of net asset acquired goodwill is not amortized but is reviewed for potential impairment on an annual basis or when event or circumstance indicate potential impairment at the reporting unit level reporting unit is business segment or one level below business segment the corporation ass the fair value of each reporting unit against it carrying value including goodwill measured by allocated equity for purpose of goodwill impairment testing the corporation utilizes allocated equity proxy for the carrying value of it reporting unit allocated equity in the reporting unit is comprised of allocated capital plus capital for the portion of goodwill and intangible specifically assigned to the reporting unit in performing it goodwill impairment testing the corporation first ass qualitative factor to determine whether it is more likely than not that the fair value of reporting unit is le than it carrying value qualitative factor include among other thing macroeconomic condition industry and market consideration financial performance of the respective reporting unit and other relevant entity and reporting unit specific consideration if the corporation concludes it is more likely than not that the fair value of reporting unit is le than it carrying value quantitative assessment is performed the corporation ha an unconditional option to bypass the qualitative assessment for any reporting unit in any period and proceed directly to performing the quantitative goodwill impairment test the corporation may resume performing the qualitative assessment in any subsequent period when performing the quantitative assessment if the fair value of the reporting unit exceeds it carrying value goodwill of the reporting unit would not be considered impaired if the carrying value of the reporting unit exceeds it fair value goodwill impairment loss would be recognized for the amount by bank of americawhich the reporting unit allocated equity exceeds it fair value an impairment loss recognized can not exceed the amount of goodwill assigned to reporting unit an impairment loss establishes new basis in the goodwill and subsequent reversal of goodwill impairment loss are not permitted under applicable accounting guidance for intangible asset subject to amortization an impairment loss is recognized if the carrying value of the intangible asset is not recoverable and exceeds fair value the carrying value of the intangible asset is considered not recoverable if it exceeds the sum of the undiscounted cash flow expected to result from the use of the asset intangible asset deemed to have indefinite useful life are not subject to amortization an impairment loss is recognized if the carrying value of the intangible asset with an indefinite life exceeds it fair value variable interest entitiesa vie is an entity that lack equity investor or whose equity investor do not have controlling financial interest in the entity through their equity investment the corporation consolidates vie if it ha both the power to direct the activity of the vie that most significantly impact the vie economic performance and an obligation to absorb loss or the right to receive benefit that could potentially be significant to the vie on quarterly basis the corporation reassesses it involvement with the vie and evaluates the impact of change in governing document and it financial interest in the vie the consolidation status of the vies with which the corporation is involved may change result of such reassessment the corporation primarily us vies for it securitization activity in which the corporation transfer whole loan or debt security into trust or other vehicle when the corporation is the servicer of whole loan held in securitization trust including non agency residential mortgage home equity loan credit card and other loan the corporation ha the power to direct the most significant activity of the trust the corporation generally doe not have the power to direct the most significant activity of residential mortgage agency trust except in certain circumstance in which the corporation hold substantially all of the issued security and ha the unilateral right to liquidate the trust the power to direct the most significant activity of commercial mortgage securitization trust is typically held by the special servicer or by the party holding specific subordinate security which embody certain controlling right the corporation consolidates whole loan securitization trust if it ha the power to direct the most significant activity and also hold security issued by the trust or ha other contractual arrangement other than standard representation and warranty that could potentially be significant to the trust the corporation may also transfer trading account security and afs security into municipal bond or resecuritization trust the corporation consolidates municipal bond or resecuritization trust if it ha control over the ongoing activity of the trust such the remarketing of the trust liability or if there are no ongoing activity sole discretion over the design of the trust including the identification of security to be transferred in and the structure of security to be issued and also retains security or ha liquidity or other commitment that could potentially be significant to the trust the corporation doe not consolidate municipal bond or resecuritization trust if one or limited number of third party investor share responsibility for the design of the trust or have control over the significant activity of the trust through liquidation or other substantive right other vies used by the corporation include collateralized debt obligation cdos investment vehicle created on behalf of customer and other investment vehicle the corporation doe not routinely serve collateral manager for cdos and therefore doe not typically have the power to direct the activity that most significantly impact the economic performance of cdo however following an event of default if the corporation is majority holder of senior security issued by cdo and acquires the power to manage it asset the corporation consolidates the cdo the corporation consolidates customer or other investment vehicle if it ha control over the initial design of the vehicle or manages the asset in the vehicle and also absorbs potentially significant gain or loss through an investment in the vehicle derivative contract or other arrangement the corporation doe not consolidate an investment vehicle if single investor controlled the initial design of the vehicle or manages the asset in the vehicle or if the corporation doe not have variable interest that could potentially be significant to the vehicle retained interest in securitized asset are initially recorded at fair value in addition the corporation may invest in debt security issued by unconsolidated vies fair value of these debt security which are classified trading account asset debt security carried at fair value or htm security are based primarily on quoted market price in active or inactive market generally quoted market price for retained residual interest are not available therefore the corporation estimate fair value based on the present value of the associated expected future cash flow fair valuethe corporation measure the fair value of it asset and liability where applicable in accordance with accounting guidance that requires an entity to base fair value on exit price under this guidance an entity is required to maximize the use of observable input and minimize the use of unobservable input in measuring fair value under applicable accounting standard fair value measurement are categorized into one of three level based on the input to the valuation technique with the highest priority given to unadjusted quoted price in active market and the lowest priority given to unobservable input the corporation categorizes it fair value measurement of financial instrument based on this three level hierarchy level quoted price in active market for identical asset or liability level asset and liability include debt and equity security and derivative contract that are traded in an active exchange market well certain treasury security that are highly liquid and are actively traded in otc market level input other than level price such quoted price for similar asset or liability quoted price in market that are not active or other input that are observable or can be corroborated by observable market data for substantially the full term of the asset or liability level asset and liability include debt security with quoted price that are traded le frequently than exchange traded instrument and derivative contract where fair value is determined using pricing model with input that are observable in the market or can be derived principally from or corroborated by observable market data this category generally includes government and bank of america mortgage backed mb and asset backed security ab corporate debt security derivative contract certain loan and lhfs level input that are supported by little or no market activity and that are significant to the overall fair value of the asset or liability level asset and liability include financial instrument for which the determination of fair value requires significant management judgment or estimation the fair value for such asset and liability is generally determined using pricing model discounted cash flow methodology or similar technique that incorporate the assumption market participant would use in pricing the asset or liability this category generally includes retained residual interest in securitizations consumer msrs certain ab highly structured complex or long dated derivative contract certain loan and lhfs irlcs and certain cdos where independent pricing information can not be obtained for significant portion of the underlying asset income taxesthere are two component of income tax expense current and deferred current income tax expense reflects tax to be paid or refunded for the current period deferred income tax expense result from change in deferred tax asset and liability between period these gross deferred tax asset and liability represent decrease or increase in tax expected to be paid in the future because of future reversal of temporary difference in the base of asset and liability measured by tax law and their base reported in the financial statement deferred tax asset are also recognized for tax attribute such net operating loss carryforwards and tax credit carryforwards valuation allowance are recorded to reduce deferred tax asset to the amount management concludes are more likely than not to be realized income tax benefit are recognized and measured based upon two step model first tax position must be more likely than not to be sustained based solely on it technical merit in order to be recognized and second the benefit is measured the largest dollar amount of that position that is more likely than not to be sustained upon settlement the difference between the benefit recognized and the tax benefit claimed on tax return is referred to an unrecognized tax benefit the corporation record income tax related interest and penalty if applicable within product or when it acknowledges affirms settle and clear transaction and or submits trade information to the appropriate clearing broker certain customer pay brokerage clearing and or exchange fee imposed by relevant regulatory body or exchange in order to execute or clear trade these fee are recorded net and are not reflected in the transaction price the corporation is an agent for those service investment banking incomeinvestment banking income includes underwriting income and financial advisory service income underwriting consists of fee bank of americaearned for the placement of completed the underwriting fee are recognized the corporation incurs certain out of pocket expense such legal cost in performing these service these expense are recovered through the revenue the corporation earns from the customer and are included in operating expense syndication fee represent fee earned the agent or lead lender responsible for structuring arranging and administering loan note summary of significant accounting principle allowance for credit lossesthe allowance for credit loss is estimated using quantitative and qualitative method that consider variety of factor such historical loss experience the current credit quality of the portfolio and an economic outlook over the life of the loan qualitative reserve cover loss that are expected but in the corporation assessment may not be adequately reflected in the quantitative method or the economic assumption the corporation incorporates forward looking information through the use of several macroeconomic scenario in determining the weighted economic outlook over the forecasted life of the asset these scenario include key macroeconomic variable such gross domestic product unemployment rate real estate price and corporate bond spread the scenario that are chosen each quarter and the weighting given to each scenario depend on variety of factor including recent economic event leading economic indicator internal and third party economist view and industry trend for more information on the corporation credit loss accounting policy including the allowance for credit loss see note summary of significant accounting principle the december estimate for allowance for credit loss wa based on various economic scenario including baseline scenario derived from consensus estimate an adverse scenario reflecting an extended moderate recession downside scenario reflecting persistent inflation and interest rate above the baseline scenario tail risk scenario similar to the severely adverse scenario used in stress testing and an upside scenario that considers the potential for improvement above the baseline scenario the overall economic outlook is weighted percent towards recessionary environment in with continued inflationary pressure leading to lower gdp and higher unemployment rate expectation compared to the prior year the weighted economic outlook assumes that the average unemployment rate will be above five and half percent by the fourth quarter of and will slowly decline to five percent by the fourth quarter of additionally in this economic outlook gross domestic product is forecasted to contract at percent and grow at percent year over year in the fourth quarter of and for comparison of december the weighted economic outlook for the average unemployment rate wa forecasted to be above five percent by the fourth quarter of and slowly decline to just under five percent by the fourth quarter of and gross domestic product wa forecasted at percent and percent year over year in the fourth quarter of and the allowance for credit loss at december wa billion an increase of million compared to december the increase in the allowance for credit loss wa primarily driven by loan growth and dampened macroeconomic outlook partially offset by reserve release for reduced pandemic uncertainty the change in the allowance for credit loss wa comprised of net increase of million in the allowance for loan and lease loss and an increase of million in the reserve for unfunded lending commitment the increase in the allowance for credit loss wa attributed to increase in the credit card and other consumer portfolio of million and commercial portfolio of million partially offset by decrease in the consumer real estate portfolio of million the provision for credit loss for credit loss december note securitizations and other variable interest entitiesthe corporation utilizes vies in the ordinary course of business to support it own and it customer financing and investing need the corporation routinely securitizes loan and debt security using vies source of funding for the corporation and mean of transferring the economic risk of the loan or debt security to third party the asset are transferred into trust or other securitization vehicle such that the asset are legally isolated from the creditor of the corporation and are not available to satisfy it obligation these asset can only be used to settle obligation of the trust or other securitization vehicle the corporation also administers structure or invests in other vies including cdos investment vehicle and other entity for more information on the corporation use of vies see note summary of significant accounting principle the table in this note present the asset and liability of consolidated and unconsolidated vies at december and in situation where the corporation ha continuing involvement with transferred asset or if the corporation otherwise ha variable interest in the vie the table also present the corporation maximum loss exposure at december and resulting from it involvement with consolidated vies and unconsolidated vies in which the corporation hold variable interest the corporation maximum loss exposure is based on the unlikely event that all of the asset in the vies become worthless and incorporates not only potential loss associated with asset recorded on the consolidated balance sheet but also potential loss associated with off balance sheet commitment such unfunded liquidity commitment and other contractual arrangement the corporation maximum loss exposure doe not include loss previously recognized through write down of asset the corporation invests in ab issued by third party vies with which it ha no other form of involvement and enters into measurementsunder applicable accounting standard fair value is defined the exchange price that would be received for an asset or paid to transfer liability an exit price in the principal or most advantageous market for the asset or liability in an orderly transaction between market participant on the measurement date the corporation determines the fair value of it financial instrument under applicable accounting standard that require an entity to maximize the use of observable input and minimize the use of unobservable input the corporation categorizes it financial instrument into three level based on the established fair value hierarchy and conduct review of fair value hierarchy classification on quarterly basis transfer into or out of fair value hierarchy classification are made if the significant input used in the financial model measuring the fair value of the asset and liability become unobservable or observable in the current marketplace for more information regarding the fair value hierarchy and how the corporation measure fair value see note summary of significant accounting principle the corporation account for certain financial instrument under the fair value option for more information see note fair value option valuation techniquesthe following section outline the valuation methodology for the corporation asset and liability while the corporation belief it valuation method are appropriate and consistent with other market participant the use of different methodology or assumption to determine the fair value of certain financial instrument could result in different estimate of fair value at the reporting date during there were no significant change to valuation approach or technique that had or are expected to have material impact on the corporation consolidated financial position or result of operation trading account asset and liability and debt securitiesthe fair value of trading account asset and liability are primarily based on actively traded market where price are based on either direct market quote or observed transaction the fair value of debt security are generally based on quoted market price or market price for similar asset liquidity is significant factor in the determination of the fair value of trading account asset and liability and debt security market price quote may not be readily available for some position such position within market sector where trading activity ha slowed significantly or ceased some of these instrument are valued using discounted cash flow model which estimate the fair value of the security using internal credit risk and interest rate and prepayment risk model that incorporate management best estimate of current key assumption such default rate loss severity and prepayment rate principal and interest cash flow are discounted using an observable discount rate for similar instrument with adjustment that management belief market participant would consider in determining fair value for the specific security other instrument are valued using net asset value approach which considers the value of the underlying security underlying asset are valued using external pricing service where available or matrix pricing based on the vintage and rating situation of illiquidity generally are triggered by the market perception of credit uncertainty regarding single company or specific market sector in these instance fair value is determined based on limited available market information and other factor bank of america from reviewing the issuer financial statement and change in credit rating made by one or more rating agency derivative asset and liabilitiesthe fair value of derivative asset and liability traded in the otc market are determined using quantitative model that utilize multiple market input including interest rate price and index to generate continuous yield or pricing curve and volatility factor to value the position the majority of market input are actively quoted and can be validated through external source including broker market transaction and third party pricing service when third party pricing service are used the method and assumption are reviewed by the corporation estimation risk is greater for derivative asset and liability position that are either option based or have longer maturity date where observable market input are le readily available or are unobservable in which case quantitative based extrapolation of rate price or index scenario are used in determining fair value the fair value of derivative asset and liability include adjustment for market liquidity counterparty credit quality and other instrument specific factor where appropriate in addition the corporation incorporates within it fair value measurement of otc derivative valuation adjustment to reflect the credit risk associated with the net position position are netted by counterparty and fair value for net long exposure is adjusted for counterparty credit risk while the fair value for net short exposure is adjusted for the corporation own credit risk the corporation also incorporates fva within it fair value measurement to include funding cost on uncollateralized derivative and derivative where the corporation is not permitted to use the collateral it receives an estimate of severity of loss is also used in the determination of fair value primarily based on market data loan and loan commitmentsthe fair value of loan and loan commitment are based on market price where available or discounted cash flow analysis using market based credit spread of comparable debt instrument or credit derivative of the specific borrower or comparable borrower result of discounted cash flow analysis may be adjusted appropriate to reflect other market condition or the perceived credit risk of the borrower mortgage servicing rightsthe fair value of msrs are primarily determined using an option adjusted spread valuation approach which factor in prepayment risk to determine the fair value of msrs this approach consists of projecting servicing cash flow under multiple interest rate scenario and discounting these cash flow using risk adjusted discount rate loan held for salethe fair value of lhfs are based on quoted market price where available or are determined by discounting estimated cash flow using interest rate approximating the corporation current origination rate for similar loan adjusted to reflect the inherent credit risk the borrower specific credit risk is embedded within the quoted market price or is implied by considering loan performance when selecting comparables short term borrowing and long term debtthe corporation issue structured liability that have coupon or repayment term linked to the performance of debt or equity security interest rate index currency or commodity the fair value of these structured liability are estimated using quantitative model for the combined derivative and debt portion of the note these model incorporate observable and in some instance unobservable input including security price interest rate yield curve option volatility currency commodity or equity rate and correlation among these input the corporation also considers the impact of it own credit spread in determining the discount rate used to value these liability the credit spread is determined by reference to observable spread in the secondary bond market security financing agreementsthe fair value of certain reverse repurchase agreement repurchase agreement and security borrowed transaction are determined using quantitative model including discounted cash flow model that require the use of multiple market input including interest rate and spread to generate continuous yield or pricing action pca framework established by the banking regulator requiring bank to maintain certain level of regulatory capital ratio comprised of five category of capitalization well capitalized adequately capitalized undercapitalized significantly undercapitalized and critically undercapitalized insured depository institution that fail to meet certain of these capital level are subject to increasingly
